class="body u-stack-x-3" itemprop="reviewBody">I thought I had ordered for my delivery to occur at 7 pm, but when I received my order confirmation, it seemed to indicate an ASAP delivery.  I contacted GrubHub customer support and expressed my concern about the delivery timing.  The representative told me that she called the restaurant and confirmed the 7 pm delivery time.  Notwithstanding these assurances, the order arrived before 6 pm.  I was not ready for my order to arrive at this time and I was very disappointed that my delivery timing request was not respected.  If GrubHub can only process ASAP deliveries, any suggestion to the contrary included on the website should be removed.</p><!----><div class="review-ordered-items-list"><div class="caption
